          <script>
           $('#site-search-939651-btn').on(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function(){
        $('#site-search-939651').submit();
        return false;
    });

    $('#site-search-939651').on('submit', function(){
        // Filter query
        var sQueryFiltered = $("#site-search-939651 input[name=q]").val().replace(/\?/g, '');
    $("#site-search-939651 input[name=q]").val( sQueryFiltered );

        if( $('#site-search-939651-term').val() ){
            return true;
        }else{
            return false;
        }
    });
    
    $('.dropdown-toggle-939651').click(function(){
        setTimeout(function(){
            $('#site-search-939651-term').focus();
        }, 50);
    });

    <script>
     jQuery(document).ready(function($){
                        var sNavContainer = '#site-navbar-container';
                        var sBodyContainer = '.offcanvas-inner';
                        var sNavHeight = $(sNavContainer).height();
                        var iUnfixPoint = 0;
                        
                        if( __tnt.client.platform.ios ){
                            $(sNavContainer).addClass('affix-sticky');
                        } else {
                            $sNavScroll = false;
                            $(window).on('DOMMouseScroll mousewheel', function(e){
                                if( !$sNavScroll ){
                                    $sNavScroll = true;
                                    setTimeout(function(){
                                        var iFixPoint = $(sNavContainer).offset().top;
                                        var iCurrPoint = $(this).scrollTop();
                                        if( iCurrPoint >= iFixPoint && iCurrPoint > iUnfixPoint ){
                                            if( !$(sNavContainer).hasClass('affix') ){ 
                                                iUnfixPoint = iFixPoint;
                                                $(sNavContainer).addClass('affix').removeClass('affix-top');
                                                $(sBodyContainer).css('margin-top', sNavHeight+'px'); 
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            if( !$(sNavContainer).hasClass('affix-top') ){ 
                                                $(sNavContainer).removeClass('affix').addClass('affix-top');
                                                $(sBodyContainer).css('margin-top', 0);
                                            }
                                        }
                                        
                                        $sNavScroll = false;
                                    }, 25);
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    });
    </script>

           <div class="center-block">

            <div id="lee-deal-container">
            </div>
            <script>
             jQuery(document).ready(function($){
                function throttleIlad(func, wait){
                    var timeout;
                    return function(){
                        var context = this, args = arguments;
                        var later = function(){
                            timeout = null;
                            func.apply(context, args);
                        };
                        clearTimeout(timeout);
                        timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
                    }
                }
                var iladLoaded = false;
                var throttledIlad = throttleIlad(function(){
                    if( !iladLoaded ){
                        iladLoaded = __tnt.elementOnScreen('#lee-deal-container');
                        if(iladLoaded){
                            $('#lee-deal-container').append('<iframe src="https://omaha.scoreyourdeal.com/widgets.php?cat_id=all" width="300" height="250" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" allowtransparency="true"></iframe>');

           <script>
            jQuery(document).ready(function($){
                    var assetTracked = [];
                    var isUserAction = false;

                    function trackActive(owl){
                        if( assetTracked.length == 10 ){
                            return;
                        }else{
                            var activeThings = $(owl).find('.owl-item.active');

                            $.each(activeThings, function(index, value){
                                var assetId = $(this).find('.card').data('id');
                                var hasBeenLogged = false;
                                
                                assetTracked.forEach(function (item, index, array) {
                                    if(item == assetId){
                                        hasBeenLogged = true;
                                        return true;
                                    }
                                });
                                if( hasBeenLogged == false ){
                                    assetTracked.push(assetId);
                                    TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                                        app: 'classifieds',
                                        metric: 'featured',
                                        id: assetId
                                    });
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    }

                    window.card_carousel_939680 = $('#block-939680 .owl-carousel');

                    card_carousel_939680.on('initialized.owl.carousel', function(e){
                            trackActive(card_carousel_939680);
                        });
                    
                    
                    card_carousel_939680.owlCarousel({
                        autoplay:__tnt.client.touchOnly ? false : true,
                        autoplayTimeout:3000,
                        autoplayHoverPause:true,
                        loop:true,
                        margin:15,
                        nav:false,
                        dots:false,
                        slideBy: 'page',
                        autoHeight:false,
                        responsiveClass:true,
                        responsiveBaseElement: '#featured-classifieds-939680',
                        responsive:{
                            0:{
                                items:1,
                                stagePadding: 40,
                                nav:false
                            },
                            600:{
                                items:1
                            }
                        }
                    });

                    // bind previous click
                    $('#block-939680 .owl-carousel-control.prev').on(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function(e){
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        card_carousel_939680.trigger('prev.owl.carousel');
                        
                        isUserAction = true;
                        trackActive(card_carousel_939680);
                    });

                    // bind next click
                    $('#block-939680 .owl-carousel-control.next').on(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function(e){
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        card_carousel_939680.trigger('next.owl.carousel');
                        
                        isUserAction = true;
                        trackActive(card_carousel_939680);
                    });

                    // bind dragged
                    card_carousel_939680.on('dragged.owl.carousel', function(event){
                        isUserAction = true;
                        trackActive(card_carousel_939680);
                    });

                    // bind translated
                    card_carousel_939680.on('translated.owl.carousel', function(event){
                        if( isUserAction ){
                            trackActive(card_carousel_939680);
                            isUserAction = false;
                        }
                    });
                });
           </script>
          </div>

   __tnt.trackEvent = function(obj) {
            if (typeof obj === 'object') {
                    if (obj.category && obj.action) {
                        __tnt.googleEvent(obj);
                    } else if (obj.network && obj.socialAction) {
                        __tnt.googleSocial(obj);
                    } else if (obj.url) {
                        __tnt.googlePageView(obj);
                    }
                    if (typeof TNCMS.Tracking != 'undefined' && obj.metric) {
                        TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                            app: obj.app,
                            metric: obj.metric,
                            id: obj.uuid
                        });
                    }
            }
